<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>minion</a> (48954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1490, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lover, royal favourite, darling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:mignon.html>mignon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dainty, pleasing, gentle, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*minnju</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">love, friendship, affection, memory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*minþijō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mindijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affectionate thought, care</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*men-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to think</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>minion</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:minions.html>minions</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A loyal servant of another, usually a more powerful being.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">disciple</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">follower</span>; <i>see also</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">loyal follower</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> May-June,  Kevin <a href = vnd.unilang:heng.html>Heng</a>,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/pub/2013/3/why-does-nature-form-exoplanets-easily">Why Does Nature Form Exoplanets Easily?</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite>, volume 101, number 3, page 184:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the past two years, NASA’s Kepler Space Telescope <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> located nearly 3,000 exoplanet candidates ranging from Sub-Earth-sized <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minions.html>minions</a></b> to gas giants that dwarf our own Jupiter.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The archvillain deployed his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minions.html>minions</a></b> to simultaneously rob every bank in the city.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A sycophantic follower.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> one; one highly esteemed and favoured.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by <a href = vnd.unilang:sylvester.html>Sylvester</a> and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>'s disciple and his <a href = vnd.unilang:dearest.html>dearest</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>minion</a></b></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1605–1608</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Timon_of_Athens" class="extiw" title="w:Timon of Athens">The Life of Tymon of Athens</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act 4, scene 3]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> this the Athenian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>minion</a></b> whom the world / Voiced so regardfully?</span><dl><dl><dd><span class="e-footer"><span style="font-size:85%;"></span></span></dd></dl></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ancient form of ordnance with a calibre of about three <a href = vnd.unilang:inches.html>inches</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1647</b>,  Francis Beaumont, Philip Massinger,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Double_Marriage" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Double Marriage">The Double Marriage</a></cite> (play), published 1717, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=ArUNAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA19amp;lpg=PA19amp;dq=%22the+double+marriage%22+%22brass+minion%22amp;source=blamp;ots=VFV5mravVVamp;sig=xZo2UM4DTZm9KOd-6KnN5Jao864amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0CB8Q6AEwAGoVChMIo8GU6d-dxwIVhqQeCh32SQDVv=onepageamp;q=%22the%20double%20marriage%22%20%22brass%20minion%22amp;f=false">page 19</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Gun. My Cannons rung like Bells. Here's to my Mistress, The dainty sweet brass <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minion.html>Minion</a></b>: split their Fore-mast, She never fail'd.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> typography<span class="ib-comma">,</span> printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between nonpareil and brevier, standardized as 7-point.</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">minimum</i></span></span>.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Robert Burton and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Of philosophers and scholars priscae sapientiae dictatores, I have already <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> in general <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a>, those superintendents of <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> and learning, <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> above <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>, those refined <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:minions.html>minions</a></b> of the muses.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Favoured, beloved; "pet".
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:minnen.html>minnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">minnon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*minjōną</i>. <p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μινώταυρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Minṓtauros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μίνως</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Mínōs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">king of Crete</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
+ <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ταῦρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taûros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:minotaur.html>minotaur</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">minotaurs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Greek mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> with the head of a bull and the body of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</li>
<li>Anything resembling the Greek <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a>, whether by appearance or by strength</li></ol>
</body> 
***minpunt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a> (48953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">min-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minpunten.html>minpunten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:minpuntje.html>minpuntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Disadvantage, downside, negative characteristic.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a></a> and its antonym <a href = vnd.unilang:pluspunt.html>pluspunt</a> have almost the same meaning as <a href = vnd.unilang:nadeel.html>nadeel</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:voordeel.html>voordeel</a>, but are not used in exactly the same situations. They only apply when talking about a characteristic or aspect of something. In the sentence "<a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondervind.html>ondervind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadeel.html>nadeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>" one cannot replace <a href = vnd.unilang:nadeel.html>nadeel</a> by <a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:minpunt.html>minpunt</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:negatief.html>negatief</a> aspect, <a href = vnd.unilang:nadeel.html>nadeel</a></li></ol>
</body>

***minute.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> minute (649)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>minute</b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:natuurkunde.html>natuurkunde</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(tijdrekening)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuut.html>minuut</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>)
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>You have one minute to complete the test.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:aardrijkskunde.html>aardrijkskunde</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuut.html>minuut</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zestigste.html>zestigste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graad.html>graad</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> need to be sure these maps are accurate to within one <b>minute</b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:notulen.html>notulen</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:meervoud.html>meervoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> minutes) (<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verslag.html>verslag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijeenkomst.html>bijeenkomst</a>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mirakel.html>mirakel</a> (8828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mirakele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">miracle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mīrāculum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">object of wonder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mīror</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wonder at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mīrus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wonderful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*smei-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mei-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile, to be astonished</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:misse.html>misse</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missa</i>.

***misbruiken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misbruiken.html>misbruiken</a> (12073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mis-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bruiken</i>: bruiken <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obsolete, compare <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruiken</a></span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to misuse, to abuse <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one's power</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***misdaad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misdaad.html>misdaad</a> (1540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">misdaet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*misdād</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*missadēdiz</i> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*missa-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mis-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dēdiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a>, act</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mis-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daad.html>daad</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">misdād</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Missetat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">misdied</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">misdåd</i>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></i>.
</p>

***misdadiger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misdadiger.html>misdadiger</a> (5939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Replaced earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">misdader</i>, probably by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdadig.html>misdadig</a></i>. Thus, now analysable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdadig.html>misdadig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdadiger.html>misdadiger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdadiger.html>misdadigers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdadiger.html>misdadigertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>criminal</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***misdeed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a> (115194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdoen.html>misdede</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">misdǣd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*missadēdiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mis-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">misded</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">misdied</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdaad.html>misdaad</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Missetat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">missdåd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌹𐍃𐍃𐌰𐌳𐌴𐌸𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">missadēþs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">misdeeds</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>That which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> done that should not have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a>, ranging from any sin or moral offense to various degrees of crime.
<dl><dd><i>The petty <b>misdeeds</b> of his youth <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> back to haunt him when he <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> for political office and his character <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> smeared.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">misdemeanor</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">misdoing</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a> (115192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mis-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misfits.html>misfits</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ill-fitting garment.</li>
<li>A failure to fit well; unsuitability, disparity.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diarmaid_MacCulloch" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Diarmaid MacCulloch">Diarmaid MacCulloch</a>, <i>A History of Christianity</i>, Penguin 2010, p. 94:
<dl><dd>And the fact that Christianity's Jesus <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the resurrected Christ <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a vital point about the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></b> between the Jesus whose teachings <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> have excavated and the Church which <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> after him.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A badly adjusted person; someone unsuitable or set apart because of their habits, behaviour etc.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:amanda.html>Amanda</a> Koci, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:charlie.html>Charlie</a> Puth, <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Smith, <a href = vnd.unilang:victor.html>Victor</a> Thellm <a href = vnd.unilang:gigi.html>Gigi</a> Grombacher, Roland Spreckle (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> and music),  “So Am I”, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ava_Max" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ava Max"><a href = vnd.unilang:ava.html>Ava</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:max.html>Max</a></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Do you ever feel like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></b>?<br />Everything inside you <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dark and twisted<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, but it's <a href = vnd.unilang:okay.html>okay</a> to be different<br />'Cause <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>, so am I</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2008</b>, Adrian Blomfield, "<a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>Has</a> Russia got a new Stalin?", <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" class="extiw" title="w:The Daily Telegraph">Telegraph</a>, 1 Mar 2008 <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/1580346/Has-Russia-got-a-new-Stalin.html">Article</a>:
<dl><dd>Just to be on the safe side, the <a href = vnd.unilang:kremlin.html>Kremlin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> also banned any of Putin's serious critics from standing. Three unelectable <b><a href = vnd.unilang:misfits.html>misfits</a></b> have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> allowed to mount token challenges.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> very unhappy in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iraq" class="extiw" title="w:Iraq">Iraq</a> and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></b> in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Army" class="extiw" title="w:Army">Army</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The MBA <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></b> when stuck in a meeting with the programmers.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">badly adjusted person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See also Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:outcast.html>outcast</a> or Thesaurus:maverick</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misfit.html>misfit</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:misfits.html>misfits</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">misfitting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">misfitted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fit badly.
<dl><dd><i>His suit <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>misfitted</b> and looked awkward.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mishandelen.html>mishandelen</a> (18581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mishandelen.html>mishandelen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mis-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handelen.html>handelen</a></i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">misshandeln</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***misleiding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:misleiding.html>misleiding</a> (14014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misleiden.html>misleiden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mislead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misleiding.html>misleiding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Deception.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>19th century. Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to miss</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***missen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a> (904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*missijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meyt-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss, to go without</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spare, to afford (going without)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieve.html>Lieve</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:missen.html>missen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">typical paedagogical window message during COVID-19 measures</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dear children, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b>miss</b> you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:missie.html>missie</a> (1279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mission</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a sending, a mission</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mission</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">expense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a sending, sending away, <a href = vnd.unilang:dispatching.html>dispatching</a>, discharging, release, remission, cessation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mittō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***mister.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a> (12529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unaccented variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">master</i>, attested since the 15th century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">misters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">A title conferred on an <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> male, usually when the name <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown. Also used as a term of address, often by a parent to a young child.</span>
<dl><dd><i>You may sit here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, George Musalas Colvocoresses, <i>Four Years in the Government Exploring Expedition</i>, J. M. Fairchild amp; co., page 358:
<dl><dd>Fine day to see sights, <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>gentlemen</a>. Well, <b>misters</b>, here's the railing round the ground, and there's the <a href = vnd.unilang:paling.html>paling</a> round the tomb, eight <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> deep, six <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> long, and three <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> wide.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1908</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>Brand</a>, <i>By Wild Waves Tossed: An Ocean Love Story</i>, The McClure Company, page 90:
<dl><dd>There's only three <b>misters</b> aboard this ship, or, rather, there's only two.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1996</b>, Spice <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>), <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wannabe_(song)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wannabe (song)">Wannabe</a></i> (song)
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> help the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> who <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> between <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> and my <a href = vnd.unilang:sisters.html>sisters</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asterix_and_the_Picts" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Asterix and the Picts"><a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a> and the Picts</a></i>, page 37
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a>: What? And only now you tell us?</dd>
<dd>Obelix: I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> talking to the future queen, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a>!</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a>: And I advise you to change your tone, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> Obelix!</dd>
<dd>Obelix: The future queen and I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> need your advice, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a>! <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>Mister</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:asterix.html>Asterix</a> gives too much advice anyway!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Use of the term, enunciated with <a href = vnd.unilang:extra.html>extra</a> emphasis, may express scorn.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">misters</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mistering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mistered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To address by the title of "<a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a>".</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">myster</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mester</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:meister.html>meister</a></i> (et <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>.), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">misterium</i>, a medieval conflation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ministerium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ministry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mysterium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mystery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">misters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone's business or function; an occupation, employment, trade.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, type of.
<ul><li><b>1590</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i>The Faerie Queene</i>, I.ix:
<dl><dd>The <i>Redcrosse</i> knight toward him crossed fast, / To <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a>, what <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so dismayd<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Need (of something).
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:9.8?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter viij</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book VII:
<dl><dd>And thenne the grene knyghte kneled doune / and dyd hym homage with his swerd / thenne <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the damoisel <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> repenteth grene knyghte of your dommage / and of youre broders dethe the black knyghte / for of your <a href = vnd.unilang:helpe.html>helpe</a> I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> grete <b>myster</b> / For I drede <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> sore to <a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passe</a> this forest / Nay drede you not sayd the grene knyghte / for ye shal lodge with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> this nyghte / and to morne I shalle <a href = vnd.unilang:helpe.html>helpe</a> you thorou this forest</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Necessity; the necessary time.
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:3.13?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter xv</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book I:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> by Merlyns auyse <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the knyghte / As for hym sayd kynge Carados / I wylle encountre with kynge <a href = vnd.unilang:bors.html>bors</a> / and ye <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> rescowe <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> whan <b>myster</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> / go on <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> they <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> do all that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> may</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">misters</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mistering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mistered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be necessary; to matter.
<ul><li><b>1590</b>, Edmund Spenser, <i>The Faerie Queene</i>, III.vii:
<dl><dd>As for my name, it <b>mistreth</b> not to tell; / Call <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> the <i>Squyre of <a href = vnd.unilang:dames.html>Dames</a></i> that <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> beseemeth well.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">misters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A device that <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:sprays.html>sprays</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a>.
<dl><dd><i>Odessa D. uses a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></b> Sunday to fight the 106-degree heat at a NASCAR race in Fontana, California.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>
